  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_74719a65-baa3-4787-b7ee-e5c0a4b58580'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer4465783055847644268">This morning, Kady thought breaking up with Ezra was the hardest thing she’d have to do. Now with enemy fire raining down on them, Kady and Ezra — who are barely even talking to each other—are forced </span>
  <span id="freeText4465783055847644268" style="display:none">This morning, Kady thought breaking up with Ezra was the hardest thing she’d have to do. This afternoon, her planet was invaded.<br /><br />The year is 2575, and two rival mega-corporations are at war over a planet that’s little more than a speck at the edge of the universe. Now with enemy fire raining down on them, Kady and Ezra — who are barely even talking to each other—are forced to evacuate with a hostile warship in hot pursuit.<br /><br />But their problems are just getting started. A plague has broken out and is mutating with terrifying results; the fleet’s AI may actually be their enemy; and nobody in charge will say what’s really going on. As Kady hacks into a web of data to find the truth, it’s clear the only person who can help her is the ex-boyfriend she swore she’d never speak to again.<br /><br />Told through a fascinating dossier of hacked documents — including emails, maps, files, IMs, medical reports, interviews, and more — <i>Illuminae</i> is the first book in a heart-stopping trilogy about lives interrupted, the price of truth, and the courage of everyday heroes.</span>

<div id="review_1288475739" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1288475739" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1288475739?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1288475739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10137603940248705490">Visually, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_' title='Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman' rel='nofollow noopener'>Illuminae</a> is an extremely fun and unique kind of book. It's a romantic space opera told through a collection of interview transcripts, diary entries, emails and gorgeous space images like this:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438386547i/15701235._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sounds amazing, no? If I was rating solely based on cool ideas, this would get a bajillion stars.<br/><br/>A book this attractive should not be boring and yet the most exciting things about it - by far - were the unusual style and graphics. The story itself - of a planet being invaded in 2575 - simply didn</span>
  <span id="freeText10137603940248705490" style="display:none">Visually, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23395680.Illuminae__The_Illuminae_Files___1_" title="Illuminae (The Illuminae Files, #1) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Illuminae</a> is an extremely fun and unique kind of book. It's a romantic space opera told through a collection of interview transcripts, diary entries, emails and gorgeous space images like this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438386547i/15701235._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sounds amazing, no? If I was rating solely based on cool ideas, this would get a bajillion stars.<br><br>A book this attractive should not be boring and yet the most exciting things about it - by far - were the unusual style and graphics. The story itself - of a planet being invaded in 2575 - simply didn't hold my attention. I found myself wanting to skim read many of the pages. Maybe it was because the lovers at the centre of the novel were boring caricatures of teenagers.<br><br>Maybe it was because of the detailed scientific descriptions and diagrams of spaceships:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438388969i/15701442._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maybe it was the tiresome and dull "Unipedia" pages that made me feel like I was studying for an essay:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438388969i/15701443._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But mostly I think it was because of the teens in love. Kady embodies the definition of a "strong heroine" but doesn't actually have a personality beyond that. Her entire characterization is built around badass girl power and I almost want to love that fact, but she never felt like a person. She felt like a cardboard cutout delivering snarky toughness.<br><br>The conversations between her and Ezra feel forced, like someone reading off a script:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438389813i/15701612._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's the kind of book that looks way better from far away.<br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.org" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/EmilyMayTheBookGeek" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10137603940248705490" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1291258798" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1291258798" />
    <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies"><img alt="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500999223p2/4527753.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1291258798?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies">Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1291258798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16792508100640012257">DNF at 30%<br/><br/>This book is written in epistolary format, and it has the honor of being <b>the most annoying book I've read this year</b>. Some people love that stuff. I ain't one of them. I love space shit. Firefly. Star Wars (yes, EVEN THE NEWER ONES). Star Trek (I loved Enterprise and I don't care who knows it). This book was just terrible and terribly formatted.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447174319i/16965999.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The first few chapters are entirely interviews. It was annoying as shit. It didn't endear me to the main characters, and it explain nothing. Int</span>
  <span id="freeText16792508100640012257" style="display:none">DNF at 30%<br><br>This book is written in epistolary format, and it has the honor of being <b>the most annoying book I've read this year</b>. Some people love that stuff. I ain't one of them. I love space shit. Firefly. Star Wars (yes, EVEN THE NEWER ONES). Star Trek (I loved Enterprise and I don't care who knows it). This book was just terrible and terribly formatted.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447174319i/16965999.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first few chapters are entirely interviews. It was annoying as shit. It didn't endear me to the main characters, and it explain nothing. Interviews are nigh on useless for building a memorable introduction, unless it is in the hands of an extremely skilled writer. Not the case here.<br><br>So right off we have an annoying girl who's thinking about her ex bf when the invasion occurred (huh?). I have no idea where we are. I have no idea what year it is. I don't know what a Kerenza whatever is.<blockquote>
  <i>Interviewer: Wait, you people had a subway system? I thought this settlement was illegal?<br>Ezra Mason: Chum, the Kerenza mine operated undetected for twenty years. Whole families lived there. You know how far from the Core we are, right?</i>
</blockquote><b>WHAT. THE. FUCK. IS. GOING. ON?</b><br><br>Bad start. And it didn't get much better. After what seems like 10000000 pages of interviews, all of a sudden we're at war (still no idea where we are, what year it is, how we got here, etc.) and then young people are getting conscripted for the military.<blockquote>
  <i>Anyone showing C-grade ability or better is to be conscripted the day they hit eighteen. We need pilots. We need gunners. We need spanner monkeys and chipheads. And we need them now.<br><br>This is an unprecedented situation—to my knowledge, no stellarcorp has ever openly attacked a United Terran Authority ship. I don’t care if BeiTech Industries’ litigation department has enough red tape to gift-wrap a small moon. These corporations need to learn nobody is above the law and nobody attacks a UTA vessel without consequences.</i>
</blockquote>Yay.<br><br>There are battle ships and specs of battle ships.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447174319i/16966000.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Do I give a fuck? No, I don't. There are cool pictures. There are snippets of things I couldn't give two shits about. What I want is a sensible story, and I didn't get that here. I got a headache instead.<br><br>By 30%, I still have no idea what the fuck is going on. I concede, my brain prefers structure. If you're into this stuff, good for you. It's just not for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16792508100640012257" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2057397012" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2057397012" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2057397012?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781760113803" href="/book/show/25524728-illuminae">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2057397012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7397757919466246380"><i>”You picked a hell of a day to dump me, Kades.”</i><br/><br/>I swear the interviews with those two at the beginning of the book are certainly among the best introductions to a new series I ever read. I mean OMG!!!<br/><br/><u>
  <b>THIS BOOK!!!</b>
</u><br/><br/>I’m still not over it!! I swear when I started to read it I really didn’t know a lot about “Illuminae”. There were only three things I knew and I had absolutely no idea how it would work out for me.<br/><br/>1.) It’s a sci-fi series.<br/>2.) The format is kinda weird and apparently the audio book is</span>
  <span id="freeText7397757919466246380" style="display:none"><i>”You picked a hell of a day to dump me, Kades.”</i><br /><br />I swear the interviews with those two at the beginning of the book are certainly among the best introductions to a new series I ever read. I mean OMG!!!<br /><br /><u>
  <b>THIS BOOK!!!</b>
</u><br /><br />I’m still not over it!! I swear when I started to read it I really didn’t know a lot about “Illuminae”. There were only three things I knew and I had absolutely no idea how it would work out for me.<br /><br />1.) It’s a sci-fi series.<br />2.) The format is kinda weird and apparently the audio book is the shit!<br />3.) The hype around it is so real that it’s almost a physical thing.<br /><br />Well, enough reasons to pick up the book and to give it a try, right? If only I would have known what I was signing up to. *lol* Nothing, really <b>NOTHING</b> prepared me for the things that were about to come. I was totally swept away by this book and its events and yet… yet there were many typical tropes I already read about a thousand times. <br /><br />BUT tell you what?! It worked!!! And damn did it work!!! I dunno how Jay Kristoff and Amie Kaufmann did it but this was so, so, SO GOOD!!! The suspense was killing me and whenever I had to stop to read all I wanted to do was to continue. I mean a virus outbreak in one of the ships… My first reaction was “Been there, done that, got the freaking t-shirt”, but WOW once you dive into the story, once you get used to the format it’s almost like you’re actually there, like you’re fighting alongside Ezra and Kady and this was just awesome!<br /><br /><i>”The victim often seeks physical comfort (hand holding, embraces), ultimately increasing the chances of spreading infection. It’s genius, really. Awful, horrifying genius.”</i><br /><br />I think you can already tell that I’m struggling for words. It’s so hard to put this experience into coherent sentences! All I can say is that this book is swallowing you whole and then spits you out at the most crucial point. And there were plot twists!!! JEEZ!! Were there plot twists! The kind of plot twists that turn your entire world upside down and leave you gasping on the ground! <br /><br /><b>I <br />WAS<br />NOT <br />PREPARED<br />FOR <br />THIS!!</b><br /><br />The best thing about the entire book were the characters though. They made it all so authentic and realistic and I found myself hoping they would make it while I sent prayers into thin air. Which should give you a good impression about how attached I got to them. Plus I had a crush on all three of them! I love Kady and Ezra and <u>
  <b>I ADORE, I ABSOLUTELY ADORE AND LOVE AIDAN!!!! </b>
</u>&lt;3333<br />And their conversations! Their humour and easy banter, the bitter truth that was hidden within it so casually. This was nothing but awesome! Let me introduce those three! <br /><br /><b>The characters:</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Beware! You’re entering my characters section now and there might be spoilers ahead of you. Either you rearrange your course or you head straight into unknown non-terrestrial territory. ;-P</b>
</u><br /><br /><b>Ezra:</b><br /><br /><i>”That’s so not your business it almost punches clean past the event horizon of Not Your Business and becomes Your Business again.”</i><br /><br />Haha! Oh gosh, I loved him from the very first moment I read about him. This boy was such a precious snowflake and he had a mouth on him! *LOL* I lived and breathed for the moments he appeared. He was really such a sweet guy and behind all the cussing and swearing he was a real romantic! &lt;3 I can understand why he loved Kady and their relationship was amazing. They were friends and lovers and all I wanted for them was to be happy and to see each other again. <br /><br /><i>”Okay, well for the benefit of the sight-impaired, I am now raising my … oh, dear… yes, it’s my middle finger at Mr. Postgrad here.”</i><br /><br /><i>”All he thinks of amid this loveless dance, all he cares about here on the edge of forever, is HER. He does not want to die. Not because he is afraid. Simply because he cannot bear the thought of leaving her behind. And there, in that tiny moment, I envy him.”</i><br /><br /><b>Kady:</b><br /><br /><i>”If I lose Ezra too, it’ll be one body blow too many. <br />If I lose Ezra too, I’ll give up.<br />I don’t think I have anyone else left.<br />But while I have him, I’ll fight tooth and nail to keep us safe. Whatever it takes.”</i><br /><br />Kady! *sighs deeply* Wow! Just wow! I rarely read about such a fierce heroine and despite being so small she was so brave and <b>A.M.A.Z.I.N.G</b>!!! I mean she literally took it up with the entire world and nothing, really nothing that happened ever managed to get her down! She got up time and again and she never stopped fighting! That inner strength and iron will! *whistles* I guess I was a goner the moment she appeared in the book. &lt;333 I love my precious girl and she needs to be protected at all costs! (She’d probably kick my behind for that statement though. *lol*)<br /><br /><i>”She is a tief. A whisper.<br />Melting through curtains of code and shadow <br />Like a knife through black water.</i><br /><br /><i>”ByteMe: see u soon<br />ByteMe: or die trying<br />ByteMe: haha”</i><br /><br /><b>AIDAN:</b><br /><br /><i>”And now, with no other option, <br />They have turned to me. <br />Plucked me back from the black they left me in.<br />Thinking I will save them.”</i><br /><br />And here comes the character I truly loved the most! AIDAN the AI!!! Yes, you read right! I absolutely loved and adored AIDAN!!! <b>GAH</b>! I worship AIDAN! I’m utterly and deeply in love with him/her/it! I carry a torch for AIDAN! I’m so besotted with this AI, it’s not even normal anymore! *lol* AIDAN was such a deep character and so very, very human! This AI had such a beautiful soul! I loved every single word he/she/it thought and said. And I really dunno what this says about me. *lol* My buddy and I even wondered if this makes me AI-phile or robo-phile?! XD Is there even a word for the state of falling in love with an AI? I can’t even tell you what made me fall head-over-heels for AIDAN but I guess it was the amazing mixture of a morally grey character that only wants the best for his people but choses the wrong means to achieve that goal. All I know is that I love AIDAN and that I really, really hope to see more of him in the next book! &lt;333<br /><br />Funnily enough I read the interview with Amie and Jay at the end of the book and Jay explained his feelings about AIDAN like that: <i>”I think it’s the deepest character I’ve ever written, which is odd considering it’s a machine. I dunno what it says about me that the mass-murdering artificial intelligence affected me the most. Nothing good, probably.”</i><br /><br />Haha! I can relate to that statement so much! SAME, Jay! SAME! XD <br /><br /><i>”Perhaps bravery is simply the face humanity wraps around its collective madness.”</i><br /><br /><i>”Before this moment, I have never wished <br />To be something other than what I am.<br />Never felt so keenly the lack of hands with which to <br />Touch, the lack of arms with which to hold.”</i><br /><br /><i>”How many people have loved only to have lost?<br />How countless, the hopes that have died?”</i><br /><br /><b>Conclusion:</b><br /><br />I loved this book with every fibre of my heart. There was never a dull moment; I was constantly on the edge of my seat and I bit my thumbnail about a thousand times. *lol* If there ever was a definition of suspense you’d probably find a picture of <b>“Illuminae”</b> next to the word in the dictionary. Yes, it was that good! ;-) If you’re still hesitating to read this book just because of the strange format: Just pick it up! Read it! Feel it! Get swept away in the tide and enjoy that freaky outer space ride! You won’t regret it! XD<br /><br />And last but not least I want to thank <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/91677980-craig" rel="nofollow noopener">my witchling</a> for that super amazing buddy read! We’re one of the best buddy read teams ever and I can’t wait to dive into <b>“Gemina”</b> with you! I enjoyed this br so much! It was a lot of fun to guess the outcome of the ending and to wonder about what would happen next and I’m so glad we decided to read this together! To another hundred buddy reads with you. ;-P (Did you really think I’d let you off the hook?! *lol*)</span>
  <a data-text-id="7397757919466246380" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6079298875875064525">im not a fan of audiobooks, but re-reading this while listening to the audio was such a cool experience. it just added another layer to an already immersive book. 10/10 would recommend.<br/>____________________________<br/><br/>this is, hands down, one of the most unique and exciting books i have ever read. like, how cool is the format?! hacked emails, court marshal documents, security surveillance, case files, and stunning artwork. i am absolutely blown away by the level of detail in this work of genius! i ca</span>
  <span id="freeText6079298875875064525" style="display:none">im not a fan of audiobooks, but re-reading this while listening to the audio was such a cool experience. it just added another layer to an already immersive book. 10/10 would recommend.<br />____________________________<br /><br />this is, hands down, one of the most unique and exciting books i have ever read. like, how cool is the format?! hacked emails, court marshal documents, security surveillance, case files, and stunning artwork. i am absolutely blown away by the level of detail in this work of genius! i cant even imagine the amount of effort that went into creating this. <br /><br />it is safe to say that i have not, and will never, read a book as involved as this. i felt so engaged throughout it and the plot itself was sooo thrilling. it was the right amount of sci-fi, thriller, and teen love/drama. <br /><br />i. am. obsessed. <br /><br /><b>↠ <i>5 stars</i></b></span>

    <a title="chai ♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42130592-chai"><img alt="chai ♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603167303p2/42130592.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1977287716?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="chai ♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="chai ♡" href="/user/show/42130592-chai">chai ♡</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781760113803" href="/book/show/25524728-illuminae">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42130592-chai?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42130592-chai?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42130592-chai?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42130592-chai?shelf=ya-sff">ya-sff</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1977287716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1352793689091392155">Not to be dramatic but I feel like I've just went through 9 different emotions within the last two minutes and at any given moment now, I'm going to explode and become an entire fucking solar system.<br/><br/>Anyway, I'm sorry this review is a mess but since I can't even write bad poetry in an attempt to get my feelings outside of myself and until the universe sends me my next favorite person so I can unload all my emotional baggage on them...this hellsite will have to do.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“The universe owes you nothing</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1352793689091392155" style="display:none">Not to be dramatic but I feel like I've just went through 9 different emotions within the last two minutes and at any given moment now, I'm going to explode and become an entire fucking solar system.<br /><br />Anyway, I'm sorry this review is a mess but since I can't even write bad poetry in an attempt to get my feelings outside of myself and until the universe sends me my next favorite person so I can unload all my emotional baggage on them...this hellsite will have to do.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“The universe owes you nothing, Kady. It has already given you everything, after all. It was here long before you, and it will go on long after you. The only way it will remember you is to do something worth remembrance.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● First of all, I want you guys to know that the only thing that is constant in my life is <b>my love for this series</b>....<i>and</i> my ability to fall back on “sorry just got your text” but anyway<br />● with that being said, I feel like we should collectively admit how scary it is reading this book when you have no skills and no passions and when you want to Do something but mainly, you really just want to lie down… doing <i>nothing</i><br />● like, I just realized that I’m not really adding anything to the universe or anyone’s individual experience, I’m basically just racking up the water bill<br />● but these kids? <b>they know how to use missiles, fly rockets, hack computers and dezombie giant spaceships while also going through break ups and heartaches and all kind of interpersonal problems </b><br />● this is just my humble opinion but you guys are literally just 17 years old. Your life should only revolve around two things: 1) single-handedly sabotaging your social and academic life and 2) figuring out how to take naps without <i>accidentally</i> time travelling to 2025<br />● seriously, I have an unbecoming resentment towards anyone around my age who is doing something productive with their talents, fictional or not, and therefore I feel personally attacked by this book<br />● I mean explain this: it was basically the apocalypse, right? guess how many characters stopped to think, ‘you know what time it is? Time to steal clothes without worrying about the retail workers whose jobs I might be putting in jeopardy or small business owners’ <br />● <b>ZERO!!</b> which makes me wonder....are you fucking kidding me??<br />● anyway, the moral of this story kids is: if you ever feel hopeless, go outside and lay in the grass and feel the coolness of the dew on your skin and look at the sky and breathe deeply… you are not alone…there’s a pink haired eighteen years old and her artificial intelligence best friend up there fighting a maniac organization that invaded her planet and I guarantee you they are <b>IN DEEPER SHIT</b><br />● <br />● ok, the characters<br />● honestly, I love every single one of these characters and I am so sick of my weak disintegrating body I need to become strong enough to lift them, their family and potential pets with one hand and carry them across space......since you know, people tend to die in this book<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>-KADY GRANT:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I am frequently underestimated. I think it's because I'm short.” </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● I want to be someone else but kady grant is already taken and I'm not creative enough to become my own person<br />● kady is… how do you say… beautiful strong amazing capable badass powerful gorgeous stunnig effervescent ethereal and an angel like being<br />● whenever I see a fanart/edit of her, I immediately die for two seconds before she gently floats down and revives me and softly wipes my gay tears while playing the lyre<br />● I just love her so much I wish we could get married so we can use glittery rose gold wax to seal our invites<br />● and honestly I wish I had the sheer will of force to be <i>her</i> because it was amazing how she got through everything she didn’t think she was strong enough for<br />● even though her bravery was bordering on insanity and half the time, I was just like, what is she doing!!! what is she attempting to accomplish!!! what is she coercing from her soul!!! why would she cosign on this spiritual monstrosity!! STOP HER!!!<br />● also, girls with pastel hair make me weak in the knees so I might be slightly biased<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>- EZRA MASON:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />● alright, here’s the thing: I really can’t choose between wanting to punch him and wanting to cradle him in my arms and protect him from all harm. it’s like trying to decide whether to have pizza or pasta… you never turn down double carbs!!!<br />● I feel like if Ezra were a real life person, he’d be tragically undateable to the masses. You would go on a dinner date with him and get drunk and share a spaghetti strand but you would never want to see him again<br />● he’s the kind of person who would say ‘uuh one second has passed’ when you go ‘just give me a sec’ <br />● you know exactly that type (aka, the type you need to avoid and sacrifice to the aztec gods)<br />● he <i>is</i> kind of annoying but I love him..... and if you think that I will forever look for any excuse, any opportunity to be as inconsistent as possible in all endeavors of my life always, you are most definitely correct<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>- AIDAN:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Am I not merciful?” </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● ah yes, the arrogant mass-murdering psychopathic part time tortured poet giant calculator… how I’ve missed it<br />● so arrogant in fact that he would give Julius Caesar a run for his money<br />● you know Julius Caesar…the same dude who was kidnapped by the cicilian pirates and when they demanded a ransom of 620 kgs of silver, he got really angry because he thought he was worth more than that and actually made them raise it to 1550 kg??<br />● uh-uh<br />● so hey, @scientists who are actively trying to make computers learn human behavior and generally scream in existential horror, this is why you need to Stop.<br />● I mean as appealing as it is to have an artificial intelligence software in the form of like, a really smooth orb for company, or even… saaay uploading your consciousness into a computer…that shit is too dangerous to mess with (refer to the ‘mass-murdering’ part)<br />● <b>now back to fiction</b>, AIDAN is the kind of character you love to hate but also…hate that you…lowkey…love them<br />● you know they’re Bad, and even if sometimes that little light escapes the darkness of their heart…they catch it again<br />● meaning: god is he messed up<br />● but you know what? the smell of burnt toast is so good sometimes... guess things are better when charred beyond recognition of their ideals <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>- KADY &amp; AIDAN:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Are you afraid?"<br />"Yes."<br />"Energy never stops, remember. It just changes forms."<br />"I am still afraid.” <i></i></i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● lbr, this duo is even more iconic than if dwayne “the rock” johnson was cast as sherlock holmes and vin diesel as watson<br />● they’re like… a fairy queen and a princess who work together to save a magical tree or something<br />● they are such a power couple I cannot wait for them to bring about world peace and destroy the beitech killing squad<br />● I mean, personally, I know I’d have way more self esteem if I had an artificial intelligence for a best friend that's for sure<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>- KADY &amp; EZRA:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She is catalyst.<br />She is chaos.<br />I can see why he loves her.” </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● no offense but if my partner doesn’t sacrifice themselves to save me from Zombie Island, do we even need these rings??<br />● I feel like ez and kady are that kind of couple where person A sends healthy relationship memes to person B who makes fun of them for being lame for but secretly saves to their phone<br />● you know... that disgustingly cute couple you cannot stand but also lowkey wanna have what they have??<br />● anyway, romantic love is fake but *lowers my reading glasses* I'm willing to admit I ship them for a million dollars...just saying<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>- JIMMY:</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <i>'I just want to be me at the end, you know?'</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />● LISTEN<br />● james mcnulty is my favorite everything in this book and NO, this has nothing to do with the fact that I sometimes choose the least popular characters as my favorites because my borderline ass can’t handle the idea of other people liking them as much as I do<br />● it’s like being a proud mother at a school play and cheering every time your kid comes on stage even though they’re playing the part of tree number 4<br />● ok yeah maybe it has a little something to do with it but LISTEN<br />● I love jimmy so much, even the mention of his name feels like someone’s actively scraping out my insides with a melon baller<br />● uuuh…shit…I fear my tears may drown some of the front row again<br />● but you know, they always say to Be Yourself, I guess I came into this world crying and I am never too far from my roots <br />● also, <b>JIMMY!! DESERVED!! BETTER!!</b><br /><br />sooo, I take it I'm right in assuming we all agree that re-reading the illuminae files was the best AND worst representation of a GREAT idea. yes? good? okay</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1162733235" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer8925545517143327160"><b>RE-READ REVIEW:</b><br/><br/>Yes yes I am officially 100% Illuminae trash and I COULD CRY BECAUSE I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH. I literally....afjkdlasfd. What am I even supposed to say here? OKAY. Just a few like "reread" thoughts in list format because that's who I am.<br/><br/>• First off <b>the audiobook is freaking amazing</b> and I CANNOT RECOMMEND IT ENOUGH. It's got tons of voices, it's basically dramatised, there is MUSIC and like beep-booping (shh, technical term there) of machines and I lovelovelovelovelove it.<br/>• The em</span>
  <span id="freeText8925545517143327160" style="display:none"><b>RE-READ REVIEW:</b><br /><br />Yes yes I am officially 100% Illuminae trash and I COULD CRY BECAUSE I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH. I literally....afjkdlasfd. What am I even supposed to say here? OKAY. Just a few like "reread" thoughts in list format because that's who I am.<br /><br />• First off <b>the audiobook is freaking amazing</b> and I CANNOT RECOMMEND IT ENOUGH. It's got tons of voices, it's basically dramatised, there is MUSIC and like beep-booping (shh, technical term there) of machines and I lovelovelovelovelove it.<br />• The emotion in the audiobook actually nearly made me CRY.<br />• Actually all the <b>intensely amazing plot twists</b> still hit me. HARD. This is also because I never remember anything of what I read??? So like it was reading a completely new book almost????<br />• And I'm quite the auditory learning, <b>so I absorbed a LOT more</b> this time. afjdaksld the plot twists.<br />• THE PLOT TWISTS THE PLOT TWISTS THE PLOT TWISTS.<br />• <b>Favourite character is: AIDAN.</b> It actually concerns me how much I love the slightly psychotic computer. But I also related to him a lot?? He predicts humans but he can't understand them. He does his best but people don't understand him. And just ajfdkslad I love AIDAN so much. I actually don't really think he's so much a villain as an anti-hero.<br />• Still shipping him and Kady. &lt;3<br />• Who is apparently said "Kady" like "Katey"?? Not "caddie"?? OKAY MY LIFE IS A LIFE.<br />• Story of Cait's Life: mispronouncing everything ever.<br />• Also why is everyone dead.<br />• why are my emotions frayed at the edges.<br />• why is the book so beautiful to look at.<br />• why was I lying on th eground listening to an audio and petting the amazing pictures in this book.<br />• help me.<br />• (except don't, I'm happy in this mindfield of pain)<br />• Also I just want to point out this has <b>one of the best romances ever and yet it's SO lowkey.</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ezra and Kady kiss ONCE in the very last chapter. And yet SHIP THIS GALACTIC EXPLOSION....I mean, yeah, I ship Kady and AIDAN. But, they can be a broship. I'll accept that too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />• Did I mention AIDAN?!?<br />• Also the plot twist that MADE ME LOSE MY MIND EVEN THOUGH I KNEW IT WAS COMING!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br />• LEAST TO SAY: this book is even better the second time. I gave it 5stars originally, but I want to give it 9384928 stars I JUST LOVE IT SO MUCH. I finished it and literally <i>ached</i> because I didn't want it to be over.<br />• One of the most special books of all time. &lt;3<br />• someone give me Gemina. I'm lying on the floor IN A PUDDLE OF EMOTION and can't get up<br /><br /><br /><b>*** ORIGINALLY REVIEWED = NOV 2015 ***</b><br />So basically....<b>FJADS28472QUIOQYQQQREUYEIP HOW DO I DO WORDS I LOVE THIS OMG. 2U18WQERWRWKLJKJ K...*collapses weeping*</b> This book is good okay? I was dubious. I spent the first, nearly, 200-pages not loving it. I was confused and then...and then. SUDDENLY I JUST ADORED EVERYTHING. <br /><br />I'm a <i>big</i> fan of books with quirky formatting and this? This takes the cake. And the tea and crumpets and planets. It's like ART as well as a book. There are pictures (!!) of the spaceships (!!!!!) and it's full of messages and transcripts and sun bursting explosions and gobs and gobs of dialogue. I <i>love</i> dialogue. And yes, it lacked description for some things..but, heck, I don't even really care about description. SO I WAS 100% OKAY WITH THAT. <br /><br /><b>Why was I confused?</b> Um. Heavy sci-fi lingo, folks. HEAVY. I still actually am unsure about a LOT of details and things, including WHY they were under attack. Yes I am a deluded pineapple brained melon. BUT. I TRY. It was just very .... difficult at times? There are blocks of text of some random people observing the main characters/events and those felt a bit dry to me.<br /><br />Buuuuut. Somehow...that all aside...I FREAKING LOVED IT?!?!?!?!??!? I CANNOT EVEN RIGHT NOW OKAY. <b>It absolutely punched me in the feels like no other.</b> And I'm squeaking because...wow. It's genius. These authors (Aussies, btw) are <i>genius</i>.<br /><br />OKAY!! But a quick overview on what the book is actually <i>about</i> for those of you who are like "Yeah, that's all well and good, CAit, but what's the freaking lump of pages about????" I shall answer thee.<br />(By the way, it totally is a brick. 600 pages and it's HEAVY. My arms hurt from reading it. #BookwormTragedy)<br /><br /><b>Small Summary Of Things In This Book:</b><br />• It is about two teens (Ezra and Kady) whose planet gets destroyed and they end up on separate getaway ships. There is another ship coming to kill them. Idek why. I didn't...get that bit. (My bad.)<br />• Kady is a hacker. (!!!!!!)<br />• Ezra is a donkey.<br />• HAHA JUST KIDDING. Ezra is adorable and kind of has violent/anger issues and is a scream.<br />• They're both really REALLY sarcastic, okay?!? Which I love.<br />• Unfortunately when the book starts they've just broken up, so they hate each other...but they also still totally love each other. So that's awkward teenage love for you.<br />• YES the book is entirely told in pictures, files, instant-message conversations, and a few chapters of description from, like, a security camera sort of thing.<br />• And it's also told from the POV of an evil computer named AIDEN who is wonderful. I love ADIEN. &lt;3 AIDEN is also a psychopath, totally, which is awkward considering I just said I love him (but forgive me) and is eeeevil as well as protectable. Whatever that means. Idek, humans, I'm doing my best. I'm fighting off a bookhangover here. I AM DRUNK ON ILLUMINAE. <br /><blockquote>[Kady] "Um, because you're loopier than Flacky McPsycho, Mayor of Crazytown?"<br />[AIDEN] "My databases show no record of this Crazytown of which you speak. A brain the size of an entire city burns inside me. My intelligence quotient is beyond the human scale. I would prefer if you did not refer to me in such a fashion."<br />"Oh, poor baby. Did I hurt the mass-murdering psychopathic artificial intelligence's feelings?"</blockquote><br />• What was I even saying? Omgooord.<br />• SO. There is tons of heavy sci-fi lingo. Sometimes I was very much like "WUT WUT WUT" but I think if you get past the first 100 or so pages you get into a flow.<br />• It gets REALLY emotional, which is hard to believe for a book that totally is functioning on messages and transcripts of documents, right?!? BUT IT DOES. <br />• The ending reduced me to a screeching wormhole of stars and glitter and terrible roaring wails. All. All of it. You see the problem here?<br />• Also there's lots of shooting and fighting and kind of an undead disease thing. <br />• And all the swear words are blanked out for "censoring", which I found a LITTLE ridiculous, but kind of quirky too? But, seriously, this book has the MOST swearing of any YA I've read, I think. o.O Just because it's blanked out ain't meaning I don't focus on it.<br />• There was a part where I howled particularly loud and considered tossing the book across my room, but a) I didn't want to break a wall because this book is so FRIKKING BIG and b) I kind of wanted to read on. #bookwormtragedies<br />• Oh and because of all the instant-messaging transcripts, there are actually typos!! I LOVE THAT. Best book ever! TYPOOOOOS. I want to write a book where I can get away with typos, gawsh darnit.<br />• I want book two.<br />• LIKE NOOOOOOOOW.<br />• And it reminded me simultaneously of Eagle Eye (fabulous movie with evil computer, go watch it now) and also Star Trek. So smush them together = Illuminae. <br /><br /><b>I really have nothing left to say except: WOW.</b> I thought I'd like it but, gawsh, those 100 first pages freaked me out that I wouldn't. I was definitely bored in some places and I missed not knowing much about the characters features. And I missed lyrical prose. There's a little? But really not much. It was a feels ride and...OH. I really want to listen to the audio book!! I've heard it's got some epic quirks too. SO BASICALLY I NEED IT NOW. This is like one of the only times I've literally put down a book and gone "yuuup but I wanna read it again". <br /><br />The hype is true, humans. THE HYPE IS TRUE. <br /><br /><blockquote> [Ezra] "you deserve every star in the galaxy laid out at your feet and a thousand diamonds in your hair. You deserve someone who'll run with you as far as and as fast as you want to. Holding your hand, not holding you back. You deserve more than I could ever give you, Kady. But I'll give you everything I can if you still want me to."</blockquote></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1791905556" />
    <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey"><img alt="Chelsea Humphrey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585613513p2/47207032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1791905556?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea Humphrey" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey">Chelsea Humphrey</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1791905556" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15765909500902144184"><b>UPDATED THOUGHTS:</b><br/>Ok, so I've calmed down a bit and am feeling better about this. It's amazing how many different forms this book took; in the beginning I was intrigued but felt it was a little slow moving, partially due to so many "technical sci-fi (ish)" terms and the choppy format. Amazing how it could feel so hindering yet unique at the same time. Once the stage was set though, I had a really hard time putting this down. I had no idea how many twists and turns I was in for, and I REALLY had n</span>
  <span id="freeText15765909500902144184" style="display:none"><b>UPDATED THOUGHTS:</b><br />Ok, so I've calmed down a bit and am feeling better about this. It's amazing how many different forms this book took; in the beginning I was intrigued but felt it was a little slow moving, partially due to so many "technical sci-fi (ish)" terms and the choppy format. Amazing how it could feel so hindering yet unique at the same time. Once the stage was set though, I had a really hard time putting this down. I had no idea how many twists and turns I was in for, and I REALLY had no idea how emotional of a ride this would be. I'm glad I put this one off until I already had <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29236299.Gemina__The_Illuminae_Files___2_" title="Gemina (The Illuminae Files, #2) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a> on hand, as I didn't realize these were more of companion novels than a linear series, as time really can't be trusted in these books. All I can say is, if by some miracle you haven't read this yet, stop reading reviews and just pick up the book! Don't let anyone ruin this for you. Also, I now understand the emotions previous readers feel while seeing the new readers status updates along the way... My poor heart is still trying to recover from the whiplash this book gave me. THANKS ALOT GUYS. <br /><br /><b>ORIGINAL THOUGHTS:</b><br />WHAT DID I JUST READ?!?!?! My feelings are feeling all of the feelies right now, and how dare you leave me hanging like that? JK, I have the next book on my shelf. My words aren't working right now, but this started out as one book and then turned into another? I feel like I've been privileged to these characters most intimate details and it makes me slightly uncomfortable in the best way. I'll think on this and try to write a real review with words and thoughts and things. MIND BLOWN. <br /><br />P.S. Please make this a movie. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15765909500902144184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1167003488152828658" style="display:none">I. <br><b>{ERROR}</b><br><br>AM. <br>IN. <br><br>LOVE.<br><b>{ERROR}</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1562280285ra/27769891.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I award one MILLION stars to <i>Illuminae</i>!!!</b><br><br>Seriously, <b>ALL THE STARS</b> go to this <u>absolute gem</u> of YA Science Fiction!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1562280285ra/27769890.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I sort of feel like I was the last person in the universe to experience <i>Illuminae</i>. <div id="review_1315348919" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1315348919" />

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45618-karen?shelf=why-yes-i-ya">why-yes-i-ya</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1315348919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3634648311833811027">holy ████████ what a ████████ fantastically fun book!<br/><br/>i have never read anything by these authors before. i was aware of kristoff's books, having put them on channels back when i was doing that sort of thing, and i knew about kaufman, but her books had never called out to me. no disrespect, but i see a cover like this:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1383578978l/13138635.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>and my first thought is "not for me." i know my own tastes, and i know that this kind of story is not likely to speak to me. <br/><br/>but this book was getting pushed so hard at BEA, i was c</span>
  <span id="freeText3634648311833811027" style="display:none">holy ████████ what a ████████ fantastically fun book!<br><br>i have never read anything by these authors before. i was aware of kristoff's books, having put them on channels back when i was doing that sort of thing, and i knew about kaufman, but her books had never called out to me. no disrespect, but i see a cover like this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1383578978l/13138635.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and my first thought is "not for me." i know my own tastes, and i know that this kind of story is not likely to speak to me. <br><br>but this book was getting pushed so hard at BEA, i was curious about it, and i'll be honest - i flipped through it and thought, "i can probably read this pretty quickly," so it got pushed to the top of the to-read stack sooner than it may otherwise have. <br><br>i don't want to give too much away, so all you need to know is that this is primarily an actiony romance that takes place in outer space told through a series of found footage, emails, schematics, internal memos, and other reports, including some pages that look like this:<br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/IMG_5390_zps7q1fjp0i.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435351427i/15338186._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_5390_zps7q1fjp0i.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/IMG_5393_zpsayelx5jk.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435351427i/15338187._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_5393_zpsayelx5jk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/IMG_5391_zpsuvjzinku.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435351427i/15338188._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_5391_zpsuvjzinku.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1131.photobucket.com/user/kettincat/media/flat%20stanley/IMG_5388_zpsofdi1dbr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435351223i/15338159._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_5388_zpsofdi1dbr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>and here's the kicker - i do not like outer space books or romance, and i am wary of ephemera-based books, having been burned too many times before. sure, there are exceptions to all rules (because -phoebe north), but i went into this as an impartial investigator - as a reviewer trying to stay on top of what is popular and what is going to be popular. <br><br>it did not grab me from the outset. there's a lot of teen-snark and flippancy, kady is SO girlpower competent and tough, ezra's supposedly witty remarks were setting my teeth on edge, and there's such a forced "look at how many women are in positions of power" show, it felt a little pandering. but that's when i was reading it as a reviewer. <br><br>there was a point where that all changed, and suddenly i was reading it in a more familiar and comfortable role - as an engaged reader; as a fan.<br><br>and it started kicking my readerly ████████.<br><br>i never did warm to the star-crossed lovers as characters, but the story itself was incredible. there is just one twist after another, and i am happy to say that i didn't see all of them coming. and one of them completely blew me away <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[which, of course, was the one that was later nullified by not actually being true and it broke my heart a little. i thought it was such a bold ballsy move and i LOVED it, so i was incredibly disappointed with the fallback into conventional YA "everything works out!" territory.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>but those are my only two gripes - not liking the characters and feeling cross at the retraction-of-ballsiness. which sounds like two things major enough to ruin the experience, but not at all, dude. this book is a gripping explosion of fun and deep space carnage, and the bonus of a kind of variation on the zombie novel. plus, AIDAN. <br><br>oh, and this:<br><br><b>am i not merciful</b><br><br>the publisher's note in the ARC predicts that this will "become <i>the</i> buzz phrase of 2015." and i hope it does. chills, my friends, chills…<br><br>it's clear just how much fun they had writing this. there are so many little subtle shout-outs to fellow-YA authors and easter eggs in the fine print - it's like being at a slumber party where you stay up all night telling scary stories that are punctuated by nervous giggles and you start getting really silly with lack of sleep and you're laughing but it's all so ████████ horrible.<br><br>i loved this book, and i am droolingly awaiting part two. <br><br>be merciful, and bring it to me quick.<br><br>************************************************************<br><br>huh. okay. now i understand why you're ballsy enough to plunge into calculated ri$k-territory to mass-produce a hardcover ARC that's nicer and more detailed than most finished books, give thousands of them away at BEA and STILL shell out for the full staircase ad: <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435187317i/15314879._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>this book's gonna sell. a lot. <br><br>it's not a perfect slam dunk, but the things i thought were thumbs-down are likely just my own personal thumbs. i will review this for real soon, but just so you know - very fun, very fast, and very unexpected.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528725630i/25720315.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://bloggycomelately.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">come to my blog!</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

And look at the inside, well one page at least...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446841512i/16910491._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Obviously you can read on the book that Kady and Ezra were living on a little planet with their parents. Kady had broken up with Ezra and then all hell breaks loose on the planet! The BeiTech Corp starts a war on the planet and everyone is trying to get to the ships to get the hell out of dodge. Kady ends up saving Ezra, but they end up on different ships when they take off. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446841512i/16910492._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kady is on the Hypatia and Ezra is on the Alexander. They are being pursued by Bei Tech's ship called Lincoln. I'm not giving out to much information on this book because I think you really need to read it. I will just tell you that a plague breaks out on their other ship called Copernicus and some of this plague gets onto the Alexander. There is also an AI on the Alexander they call Aidan and this AI goes all wackadoo and creates havoc. <br><br>I loved how the layout is in messages, files and just ahhhhhhhhh... I love it! And there is not tons of action in the book, for those that love ALL action, it's just full of so much coolness. I can't believe how happy I am to have read such an awesome sci-fi, young adult book! <br><br>*CLAPS*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446841512ra/16910493.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446841512ra/16910494.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446841512ra/16910495.gif" alt=" " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And this is a trilogy!!!! A TRILOGY!!!! Oh, I hope I don't keel over before the next two books come out! I am so excited to see if they are going to get to their destination...which I'm not telling where.. and I want to see what all is going to happen with the people that made it out alive! <br><br>I love Kady and Ezra! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446841512i/16910496._SY540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you like this type of genre just read it.. read it.. read it.. and I hope you love it as much as I do!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17666474042068757452" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1315539910" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1315539910?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=sent-from-pub">sent-from-pub</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1315539910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2071528400180965084">4.5 stars <br/><br/>This book is incredible! Definitely the most unique reading experience i've never had. It felt like you were in a video game, or watching a sci-fi movie. I absolutely love the way it was written and all the cool page designs and the way that the world is established is very immersive and you feel like you're a hacker reading into life on this spaceship. I love how the authors were able to write such a variety of different scenes and voices, for example how the Artificial Intelligence u</span>
  <span id="freeText2071528400180965084" style="display:none">4.5 stars <br /><br />This book is incredible! Definitely the most unique reading experience i've never had. It felt like you were in a video game, or watching a sci-fi movie. I absolutely love the way it was written and all the cool page designs and the way that the world is established is very immersive and you feel like you're a hacker reading into life on this spaceship. I love how the authors were able to write such a variety of different scenes and voices, for example how the Artificial Intelligence unit of the spaceship having a completely unique and separate tone than that of the sassy main character. I surprisingly really liked the hint of romance that was in this, and more than once I was giggling out loud at scenes where the characters were joking around in chat rooms. The only reason I took off a half star from this book is that because of the POV, I felt like you lost a little bit of the character descriptions and explanation of the plot. It takes a while to really figure out what's happening and in the end I was left slightly confused about what the Illuminae is, and it was hard to visualize a couple of action events due to most of the narrative taking place strictly through dialogue. But overall I highly recommend you pre-order this! I will be buying a finished copy because i'm so excited to see the pages that were incomplete in my advanced copy!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="2071528400180965084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1879957563" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1879957563" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1879957563?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1879957563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7442707740017558416">There is so much hype surrounding this book, but after seeing <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1883091198' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gemina</a> make so many of my friends' <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1834969763' rel='nofollow noopener'>"Favorite Books Published in 2016"</a> lists, I couldn't ignore this series any longer. I also knew that it was told in a multimedia format, filled with interviews and IM conversations, and that made me a little apprehensive. <b>This book was so unexpectedly addictive.</b><br/><br/>This story starts off in a much further progressed world, in both years and technology, than ours, on a hidden and secluded planet far, far a</span>
  <span id="freeText7442707740017558416" style="display:none">There is so much hype surrounding this book, but after seeing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1883091198" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a> make so many of my friends' <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1834969763" rel="nofollow noopener">"Favorite Books Published in 2016"</a> lists, I couldn't ignore this series any longer. I also knew that it was told in a multimedia format, filled with interviews and IM conversations, and that made me a little apprehensive. <b>This book was so unexpectedly addictive.</b><br><br>This story starts off in a much further progressed world, in both years and technology, than ours, on a hidden and secluded planet far, far away. Our two main protagonists, Kady and Ezra, have just broken up, and despite the awkwardness they are forced to be in class with one another. That is, until their hidden and secluded planet comes under attack, and they have to rely on each other to reach the evacuation ships. <br><br>Once safe, they are forced to board different ships, Kady on Hypatia, and Ezra on Alexander, and there is also a third ship in their fleet, Copernicus. These three ships are literally running for their lives and being pursued by an enemy battleship, the Lincoln, but they soon realize that the enemy catching up to them isn't the only thing that is putting them in danger. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456339912i/18221640._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1484698007i/21743137._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456339912i/18221639._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This story will definitely keep you on the edge of your seat, while you constantly tell yourself "just one more page" until you look at the clock and see it is 3AM. It is action packed, and the format is so easy to read, that these 600 pages will feel like 300 pages. <br><br>You won't only fall in love with Kady and Ezra, but you will also fall in love with the whole ensemble of side characters. You'll laugh and you'll cry. You'll be surprised and oh so anxious. You will feel like an absolute fool for not reading it sooner. <br><br>So why did I give this four stars? Because I couldn't help but be constantly reminded of <a href="http://store.steampowered.com/app/17470/" rel="nofollow noopener">Dead Space</a>. Don't get me wrong, this book is still completely unique in its formatting and execution, but once the very climatic parts on Alexander started happening, I kept picturing myself playing that damn video game franchise. <br><br>AIDAN was my favorite, hands down. Kudos to both of these very talent authors for making that AI seem so scary, heartbreaking, and real. His points of view made this book for me, and once we got to those points of view, I couldn't stop turning the pages. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“THE UNIVERSE OWES YOU NOTHING, KADY. IT HAS ALREADY GIVEN YOU EVERYTHING, AFTER ALL. IT WAS HERE LONG BEFORE YOU, AND IT WILL GO ON LONG AFTER YOU. THE ONLY WAY IT WILL REMEMBER YOU IS IF YOU DO SOMETHING WORTHY OF REMEMBRANCE.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I was also surprised by all the twists and turns. Like, one of them was a little predictable, but the rest honestly did blindside me, especially that ending. How could you not want to immediately pick up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1883091198" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a> after that ending? <br><br>I also feel like this book would be pretty universally liked, if you don't mind the format. Like, I would totally recommend this to everyone; Sci-Fi lover or not. My only regret is not reading it sooner, because I was scared of the hype train, but now I have Goodreads and my amazing friends to thank for another beloved book in my collection. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> </span>
  <a data-text-id="7442707740017558416" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Ryan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56788355-ryan"><img alt="Ryan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1468129599p2/56788355.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1686080149?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ryan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ryan" href="/user/show/56788355-ryan">Ryan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Basically everyone</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=feels-trip">feels-trip</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=unfinished-series">unfinished-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=november-tbr">november-tbr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56788355-ryan?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>,
