        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1686080149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1540797093707878053"><b>Actual final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/>Buddy (re)read with my girls:<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-sassy-opinionated' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jenn</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/53385361-luna' rel='nofollow noopener'>Luna</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/54010598-kazzexual' rel='nofollow noopener'>Em (Kazzexual)</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26402455-sana-khalid' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sana</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mayflower</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"AM I NOT MERCIFUL?"</i>
</b><br/><br/>This book was epic. Epic, I tell you!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471723179ra/20099013.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm a <b>huge</b> sci-fi fan. As I've mentioned a hundred times over, that stuff is my shit. (Which is why I have filled this review with completely irrelevant Doctor Who gifs, and only Doctor Who gifs. You're welcome.)<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/513234.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I think you know the drill by now: I warn the reader of the sheer multitude of gifs and fangirling coming their way, st</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1540797093707878053" style="display:none"><b>Actual final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br><br>Buddy (re)read with my girls:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35147071-jenn-sassy-opinionated" rel="nofollow noopener">Jenn</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/53385361-luna" rel="nofollow noopener">Luna</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/54010598-kazzexual" rel="nofollow noopener">Em (Kazzexual)</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26402455-sana-khalid" rel="nofollow noopener">Sana</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508" rel="nofollow noopener">Mayflower</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"AM I NOT MERCIFUL?"</i>
</b><br><br>This book was epic. Epic, I tell you!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471723179ra/20099013.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm a <b>huge</b> sci-fi fan. As I've mentioned a hundred times over, that stuff is my shit. (Which is why I have filled this review with completely irrelevant Doctor Who gifs, and only Doctor Who gifs. You're welcome.)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/513234.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I think you know the drill by now: I warn the reader of the sheer multitude of gifs and fangirling coming their way, state more than once that "this is not a review, but more of a mess of my thoughts", et cetera, et cetera.</b><br><br>Illuminae had everything I loved: brilliant storytelling, lovable characters, and a chilling, captivating plot.<br> <br><b>
  <i>"Nothing ceases to exist. Energy does not perish, it merely changes forms. The ones you love, the ones you lose, they still exist as long as the cosmos does."</i>
</b><br><br>The main reason I bought this book was because of how hyped it was on Booktube, and how <b>fucking glorious the cover is</b>. It's okay to judge a book by it's cover in this case. I was not disappointed. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471725192ra/20099255.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The characters were absolutely hilarious. One second I was stressing over the fate of the <i>Alexander</i> and the next:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471728515ra/20099665.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Discarded message:<br>Also, my friend here is wondering about the survivors lists becauseASDLKDGFKNDFGJBE MORE SUBTLE KADY LIKE A BRICK WHY DON'T YOU?"<br><br>"McNulty, J, Sgt: and if that works<br>McNulty, J, Sgt: u must name ur first kid james in my honour<br>Mason, E, LT, 2nd: &gt;_&gt;<br>McNulty, J, Sgt: if it's a daugher u name it jamette<br>Mason, E, LT, 2nd: 0_o"<br><br>"It's obvious he's got no ****ing idea what he's about - I mean, 'is in-experienced in matters of computer espionage.' (Shut up, I'm being professional.)"</i>
</b><br><br>Funnily enough, the writing style I <b>loathed</b> in Firstlife, I adored in Illuminae. It fit much better with the formatting, and didn't seem unnecessarily forced.<br><br>There were plenty of fantastic characters but my favourite had to be AIDAN. Yeah. The <b>sociopathic artificial intelligence</b> is my favourite character, and I don't know what that says about me. <s>His</s> It's scenes and back-and-forth with Kady was brilliant.<br><br><b>
  <i> AIDAN: "'DURING THE...INCIDENT... AFTERWARD, NONE OF THE MEAT HAD THE PRESCENE OF MIND TO RESTORE THE SYSTEMS DOWN THERE.'<br>Kady: 'The meat? The incident? That's what you're calling them?'<br>AIDAN: 'CALL THEM SOMETHING ELSE IF YOU WISH.'<br>Kady: 'People aren't just ****ing meat. And killing hundreds of them wasn't an incident. It was a massacre.'<br>AIDAN: 'IT WAS ALSO A NECESSITY.'<br>Kady: 'I've heard this song before.'<br>AIDAN: 'I WONDER, THEN, WHY YOU KEEP ASKING ME TO SING IT?'"</i>
</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[A part of me ships Ezra and Kady, but a part of me ships AIDAN and Kady...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471727609ra/20099554.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It is completely impossible and improbable? Yes. Does that stop a teeny-tiny part of me from shipping it? No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Now, you may be thinking, "Ryan, if you loved this book so much, why'd you give it 4 stars instead of 5?" <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471727609ra/20099555.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here comes the not-so-fangirly part of the review: There was an extreme lack of world building, and I almost lost interest towards the middle. The universe Kaufman and Kristoff created was wonderful - I wanted to know more about it, but sadly, it was never elaborated on to the degree I wished. Criticism aside, I had so much fun reading this book, and I <s>suggest</s> <i>need</i> you read it, too. <br><br><i>
  <b>Illuminae: Now run.</b>
</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1540797093707878053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2001513999?book_show_action=true">May 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2001513999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8752467919292701902">It’s true what they say. You <b>don’t need to be a fan of science fiction</b> to love this book. I, for one, am not and I could reread the hell out of this book. <br/><br/>The rumours are true. This is an <i>addictive</i> story told in letters, interviews, journal entries and other cool documentation. For creativity alone, this book deserves five full stars. <br/><br/>How convenient that Kady’s world is attacked right when she decides to break up with her boyfriend. I live for good irony. Kady and Ezra keep in touch after they b</span>
  <span id="freeText8752467919292701902" style="display:none">It’s true what they say. You <b>don’t need to be a fan of science fiction</b> to love this book. I, for one, am not and I could reread the hell out of this book. <br /><br />The rumours are true. This is an <i>addictive</i> story told in letters, interviews, journal entries and other cool documentation. For creativity alone, this book deserves five full stars. <br /><br />How convenient that Kady’s world is attacked right when she decides to break up with her boyfriend. I live for good irony. Kady and Ezra keep in touch after they both embark different ships. They help each other navigate their new environments. <br /><br />This is as much a romance as it is a science fiction story. Kady and Ezra’s flirting is so eye-roll-worthy, but a kind of eye-roll-worthy that makes you smile at the same time. I was rooting for them with much intensity. <br /><br />I do feel I had trouble connecting with characters other than the three main ones—<i>just wait until you meet the glorious Aidan!</i> It’s not that they are not present enough—though that is arguably true—; it’s that to me they were only names on paper. I barely knew anything about them, so how could I possibly get attached? Many died and I didn’t bat an eye. <br /><br />So is this a perfect book? No, definitely not. But is it enjoyable to the point of waving off its flaws? Certainly. I was intrigued, amused, mystified and charmed all at once. I could complain about other little elements, like unimportant files that could have been cut, but I don’t really want to right now. I kind of just want to dive into the sequel, if that’s okay ;)<br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>

<div id="review_1219751013" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1219751013" />
    <a title="Taneika" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika"><img alt="Taneika" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564410672p2/5591031.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1219751013?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taneika" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taneika" href="/user/show/5591031-taneika">Taneika</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781760113803" href="/book/show/25524728-illuminae">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5591031-taneika?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5591031-taneika?shelf=aussie-ya">aussie-ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1219751013" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4562723004293703865">This is one of the most hyped up books EVER so I was actually kinda hesitant to pick it up. BUT WOW. This book was absolutely wonderful. It took me a while to get into the first 100 pages or so, but after that, I absolutely flew threw it.<br/><br/>Illuminae (sorry, Illumin-YAY) consists entirely of pictures, diagrams, transcripts of recordings, interviews, instant messages, and the like. IT MADE A 600 PAGE BOOK (which I think very FEW books get away with that length) FEEL SO SHORT. <br/><br/>This is the story of a </span>
  <span id="freeText4562723004293703865" style="display:none">This is one of the most hyped up books EVER so I was actually kinda hesitant to pick it up. BUT WOW. This book was absolutely wonderful. It took me a while to get into the first 100 pages or so, but after that, I absolutely flew threw it.<br /><br />Illuminae (sorry, Illumin-YAY) consists entirely of pictures, diagrams, transcripts of recordings, interviews, instant messages, and the like. IT MADE A 600 PAGE BOOK (which I think very FEW books get away with that length) FEEL SO SHORT. <br /><br />This is the story of a teenage girl named Kady, and a boy named Ezra who, along with the rest of their planet, are forced to flee their home on Kerenza IV when a mega corporation comes along and tries to get their hands on what is being illegally mined on the tiny little planet. This mega corporation, Bei-Tech end up going after the fleets of civilians in order to destroy any evidence of them trying to illegally mine stuff. <br /><br />Okay, so that was a really shitty summary BUT IT DOESN'T MATTER BECAUSE THE CHARACTERS AND THE ATMOSPHERE YOU GET FROM THIS BOOK ARE WHAT MATTERS.<br /><br />I was unsure if I'd like Kady, I mean, the teenager who is SOMEHOW a super genius hacker??? It's a trope I'm tired of seeing and it's barely ever pulled off well. But Kady stands out from the rest, I loved how sarcastic, blunt and flawed she was, she was strong and clever and loving. Her relationship with Ezra, while starting off rocky - because they kinda broke up before their home planet was invaded - was absolutely gorgeous and heart wrenching. Yes, it was super cheesy at parts but I LIKE cheesy, and teenagers (and adults for that matter) ARE CHEESY. <br />I have to say though, my favourite character was the AI - AIDEN. I know AIDEN is a psychopathic COMPUTER but the way this freaking computer interacted with each of the characters and the dialogue between Kady and AIDEN in particular, was so well done. <br /><br />Everything in Illuminae starts off as something relatively small, and then it just grows and grows until it's blows up in your face and you're wondering how you've gone through 400 pages in what feels like an hour. Everything is incredibly atmospheric, I found myself incredibly freaked out in parts and the way this is written and put together in pieces, makes you feel so deeply involved.<br /><br />I don't know why it took me so long to pick this book up, but it was magnificent.<br /><br />For more bookish things from me, check out my Youtube channel: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/c/flippingthroughpages">https://www.youtube.com/c/flippingthr...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="4562723004293703865" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1222674063" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222674063" />
    <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes"><img alt="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598297811p2/1452829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1222674063?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~" href="/user/show/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes">Mary ~Ravager of Tomes~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=year-2017">year-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1452829-mary-ravager-of-tomes?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1222674063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13644008332652554092"><b>Surveillance footage summary,<br/>prepared by<br/>Analyst ID 8759-6294-DN</b><br/><br/>Subject known as 'Mary' is experiencing <u>high levels</u> of emotional distress while reading. Her demeanor is rapidly shifting from joy & mirth to shock & indignation and then back again. Facial expressions accordingly. Thirty minutes ago she slammed the book closed and tossed it away from her with the purest look of terror I have ever witnessed, but now she's back with her nose buried between the pages. <s>Seriously, what the ███ is wrong w</s></span>
  <span id="freeText13644008332652554092" style="display:none"><b>Surveillance footage summary,<br />prepared by<br />Analyst ID 8759-6294-DN</b><br /><br />Subject known as 'Mary' is experiencing <u>high levels</u> of emotional distress while reading. Her demeanor is rapidly shifting from joy &amp; mirth to shock &amp; indignation and then back again. Facial expressions accordingly. Thirty minutes ago she slammed the book closed and tossed it away from her with the purest look of terror I have ever witnessed, but now she's back with her nose buried between the pages. <s>Seriously, what the ███ is wrong with this ████?</s> I mean, ahem... Is the subject even enjoying her read? Sometimes it is hard for a poor data analyst to tell...<br /><br />♥ √v^‒√v^√‒√v^√v^√‒√v^√―――――――――――――――<br /><br />Ok enough messing around! Truth is, I <b>really</b> enjoyed this read.<br /><br />While the story was engrossing, it wasn't something I've never seen before. <u>The real champion of this book is the format.</u><br /><br />I am a <b>lover</b> of Science Fiction. I <b>live</b> for the spacey-wacey stuff. Spaceships &amp; science &amp; technological advancements &amp; humans contemplating their place in the cosmos. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Yes please.</i>
</b><br /><br />But never before have a seen a format so <b>unique</b> as this one. To lay out the story in the form of incident reports &amp; analyst summaries &amp; internal chat logs was <i>genius</i> in my book. <br /><br />The illustrations on each page are <b>absolutely stunning.</b> It's difficult to do something new in a time when so much as already been thought of, but <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4735144.Jay_Kristoff" title="Jay Kristoff" rel="nofollow noopener">Jay Kristoff</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5360335.Amie_Kaufman" title="Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Amie Kaufman</a> achieve a new level of individuality with <i>The Illuminae Files</i> series.<br /><br />It kept my attention locked in place, I was <b>dying</b> to turn each page and know how things would play out. There were a couple times where I feel the creator of a document has a bit more information than they're likely to (such as describing how a character on a camera feed is feeling), but it was mostly necessary to give the characters more depth.<br /><br />The pace was <b>lightning quick</b> &amp; there were moments when I felt <b>genuinely emotional</b> over the twists &amp; turns being thrown at me. A handful of really excellent characters &amp; circumstances made for a <b>very fun read!</b><br /><br /><b>**Below this point I discuss a couple spoilery things that made this a 4 star read for me instead of a 5. Click at your own risk.**</b><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br /><u><b>The Romance</b></u>:<br /><br />While individually I enjoy Kady &amp; Ezra as characters, I am not much a fan of their romance. It just feels <b>so unnecessary</b> considering everything else that's happening. They have both lost parents to the situation, the Phobos virus is turning passengers into intelligent kamikaze carriers, the <i>Lincoln</i> is in hot pursuit to destroy all survivors of the Kerenza attack &amp; cover their tracks... and I'm supposed to care about their romance? <br /><br /><b>Well I didn't.</b><br /><br />I don't know what this <b>thing</b> is with Young Adult books where we can't have a story without a damn romance. Kady &amp; Ezra aren't the worst couple I've ever read, I'm just <b>exhausted</b> with this genre forcing a romance in <u>every single book.</u><br /><br />I think I would've invested more if Kady &amp; Erza were brother &amp; sister. Maybe their parents are separated, but struggling to rekindle their love with endless miles of space between them. Maybe Ezra is ready to accept their parents getting back together but Kady isn't &amp; that's why they're fighting when the Kerenza attack occurs.<br /><br /><u>JUST ANYTHING BUT ANOTHER CHEESY ROMANCE!</u><br /><br /><u><b>The Survival</b></u>:<br /><br /><b>I'm not at all happy</b> that Ezra &amp; Kady both manage to survive this ordeal, either. If it's not miraculous enough that Ezra wasn't evacuated with his unit &amp; thus was not executed by Syra Boll, it's overkill that the <i>Hypatia</i> reversed its course &amp; located Kady's escape pod in <i>just enough</i> time to prevent the radiation poison from killing her.<br /><br />I'm glad AIDAN survived. His is the <u>only</u> survival story I can get behind, and I think it would've been <i>badass</i> for him to be the one exacting revenge against Ezra's mother &amp; BeiTech Corp. in Kady's stead.<br /><br /><u><b>The Kady Grant</b></u>:<br /><br />SO I actually <b>love</b> Kady. I love her sarcasm &amp; her intelligence &amp; her unyielding bravery. I love that if we <i>must</i> have a broken romance, it was her leaving Ezra because he couldn't give her what she needed. <b>She's a great character.</b><br /><br />My only quip with Kady is that I would've liked a little more on her tech background. <b>Just give me a believable reason she can keep up with Zhang, who's almost 30 and been studying computers for most of his adult life.</b><br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><u>I'd definitely recommend this for everyone.</u> <br /><br /><b>Even if you're not a fan of Young Adult fiction,</b> this story isn't plagued by many of the flaws of that genre. <b>Even if you're not a fan of Science Fiction,</b> the book is intelligently written without being overly complicated &amp; the pace keeps you on your toes.<br /><br />Super excited for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/29236299.Gemina__The_Illuminae_Files___2_" title="Gemina (The Illuminae Files, #2) by Amie Kaufman" rel="nofollow noopener">Gemina</a>!<br /><br /><i><a href="http://booknest.eu/reviews/34-mary-s-reviews/500-illuminae" rel="nofollow noopener">This review</a> and other reviews of mine can be found on <a href="http://booknest.eu/" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Nest</a>!</i><br /><br />Long awaited Buddy Read with my lovelies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/35431290-tweebs" rel="nofollow noopener">Tweebs</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7317186-celeste" rel="nofollow noopener">Celeste</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/54721988-ha-foun" rel="nofollow noopener">Haifa</a>!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13644008332652554092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Nat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23381142-nat"><img alt="Nat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588309995p2/23381142.jpg" /></a>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Hg1vIrBKygeJbORAHgxYjmLaPekkAvshZmR8yQLdR6D7LiyUQq/DbnwNx9rkP0jpstvNaTP2/3uCBoM0QSzs9A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PPGomYCRNl0GKhvqR13AmGyWa6XjDNANBk4c4LVVMynZ0usvcnQ/NPNLOHC9btD/vJebJfT41FfiLOMd9qSYfQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer2686237058646584746">Amie Kaufman is a New York Times and internationally bestselling author of young adult fiction. Her multi-award winning work is slated for publication in over 30 countries, and is in development for film and TV. Raised in Australia and occasionally Ireland, Amie has degrees in history, literature, law and conflict resolution. She lives in Melbourne with her husband, their rescue dog, and an extrem</span>
  <span id="freeText2686237058646584746" style="display:none">Amie Kaufman is a New York Times and internationally bestselling author of young adult fiction. Her multi-award winning work is slated for publication in over 30 countries, and is in development for film and TV. Raised in Australia and occasionally Ireland, Amie has degrees in history, literature, law and conflict resolution. She lives in Melbourne with her husband, their rescue dog, and an extremely large personal library.<br /><br />You can sign up for her newsletter to see what she's working on, hear when she releases a new book, and be automatically entered for giveaways: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.eepurl.com/6Ya8j">www.eepurl.com/6Ya8j</a><br /></span>
